x: 50-75, y: 5-11 ===\n    # Top rib / barrel shroud\n    for x in range(50, 76):\n        img.putpixel((x, 5), COLORS['black'])\n        img.putpixel((x, 11), COLORS['black'])\n    for y in range(5, 12):\n        img.putpixel((75, y), COLORS['black'])\n\n    # Barrel body\n    for y in range(6, 11):\n        for x in range(50, 75):\n            if y == 6:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_light'])\n            elif y == 10:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n            elif y == 7:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['lighter_gray'])\n            else:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_medium'])\n\n    # Ventilated rib (top of barrel) - small slots\n    for x in range(54, 73, 4):\n        img.putpixel((x, 6), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n        img.putpixel((x + 1, 6), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n\n    # Muzzle opening\n    img.putpixel((75, 7), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n    img.putpixel((75, 8), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n    img.putpixel((75, 9), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n\n    # Under-barrel lug / weight\n    for y in range(11, 14):\n        for x in range(50, 68):\n            if y == 13 or x == 50 or x == 67:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            else:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n\n    # Front sight\n    img.putpixel((72, 4), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((73, 4), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((72, 5), COLORS['lighter_gray'])\n    img.putpixel((73, 5), COLORS['lighter_gray'])\n\n    # === FRAME (upper part above cylinder) - x: 18-50, y: 4-8 ===\n    for y in range(4, 9):\n        for x in range(18, 51):\n            if y == 4 or y == 8:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            elif x == 18:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            elif y == 5:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_light'])\n            else:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_medium'])\n\n    # Rear sight\n    img.putpixel((22, 3), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((23, 3), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((24, 3), COLORS['black'])\n\n    # Hammer (exposed, at rear top)\n    img.putpixel((19, 2), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((20, 2), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((19, 3), COLORS['metal_medium'])\n    img.putpixel((20, 3), COLORS['metal_medium'])\n    img.putpixel((19, 4), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n    img.putpixel((20, 4), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n\n    # === CYLINDER (large, distinctive revolver feature) - x: 28-48, y: 8-16 ===\n    # The cylinder is the most distinctive part of a revolver\n    for y in range(8, 17):\n        for x in range(28, 49):\n            # Create rounded cylinder shape\n            cy = 12  # center y\n            cx = 38  # center x\n            ry = 4   # radius y\n            rx = 10  # radius x\n\n            # Check if point is within ellipse\n            dx = (x - cx) / rx\n            dy = (y - cy) / ry\n            dist = dx * dx + dy * dy\n\n            if dist <= 1.0:\n                if dist > 0.75:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n                elif dist > 0.6:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n                elif y <= 10:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_light'])\n                elif y >= 14:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n                else:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_medium'])\n\n    # Cylinder flutes (vertical lines showing chambers)\n    for x in [33, 36, 39, 42, 45]:\n        for y in range(9, 16):\n            cy = 12\n            ry = 4\n            dx = (x - 38) / 10\n            dy = (y - cy) / ry\n            if dx * dx + dy * dy < 0.7:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n\n    # Cylinder pin / axis\n    img.putpixel((38, 8), COLORS['lighter_gray'])\n    img.putpixel((38, 16), COLORS['lighter_gray'])\n\n    # === FRAME (lower, connecting cylinder to grip) - x: 18-30, y: 8-16 ===\n    for y in range(8, 17):\n        for x in range(18, 30):\n            if y == 16:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            elif x == 18:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            else:\n                # Only fill if not already part of cylinder\n                px = img.getpixel((x, y))\n                if px == COLORS['transparent']:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_medium'])\n\n    # === TRIGGER GUARD - x: 24-38, y: 16-20 ===\n    # Front of guard\n    img.putpixel((38, 16), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((38, 17), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((38, 18), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((38, 19), COLORS['black'])\n    # Bottom of guard\n    for x in range(24, 39):\n        img.putpixel((x, 20), COLORS['black'])\n    # Back of guard (connects to grip)\n    img.putpixel((24, 16), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((24, 17), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((24, 18), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((24, 19), COLORS['black'])\n\n    # Trigger\n    for y in range(16, 19):\n        img.putpixel((30, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n        img.putpixel((31, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n\n    # === GRIP (ergonomic rubber grip, angled back) - x: 4-18, y: 10-23 ===\n    for y in range(10, 24):\n        progress = (y - 10) / 13.0\n        offset = int(progress * 5)  # backward lean\n        gx_start = 14 - offset\n        gx_end = 20 - offset\n\n        # Grip widens slightly in the middle\n        if 3 <= (y - 10) <= 9:\n            gx_end += 1\n\n        for x in range(max(0, gx_start), min(width, gx_end + 1)):\n            if x == gx_start or x == gx_end or y == 23:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            elif (x + y) % 3 == 0:\n                # Rubber grip texture (checkered pattern)\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['grip_dark'])\n            elif (x + y) % 3 == 1:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['grip_medium'])\n            else:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['grip_light'])\n\n    # Connect grip top to frame\n    for y in range(8, 11):\n        for x in range(14, 19):\n            px = img.getpixel((x, y))\n            if px == COLORS['transparent']:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n\n    return img\n\n\ndef create_revolver_topdown():\n    \"\"\"\n    Create 34x14 top-down view RSh-12 revolver sprite.\n\n    The RSh-12 is significantly larger than the Makarov PM (30x12),\n    with a visible cylinder bulge and thicker barrel.\n    \"\"\"\n    width, height = 34, 14\n    img = Image.new('RGBA', (width, height), COLORS['transparent'])\n\n    # RSh-12 top-down layout (pointing right):\n    # [grip] [cylinder] [barrel]\n\n    # === GRIP (rubber, rear part) - x: 0-9, y: 2-11 ===\n    for y in range(2, 12):\n        for x in range(0, 10):\n            if y == 2 or y == 11:\n                if 2 <= x <= 9:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            elif x == 0:\n                if 3 <= y <= 10:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            elif x == 9:\n                if 3 <= y <= 10:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            elif y == 3 or y == 10:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['grip_dark'])\n            elif y in (4, 9):\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['grip_medium'])\n            else:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['grip_light'])\n\n    # Grip texture (checkered rubber)\n    for y in range(4, 10):\n        for x in range(2, 8):\n            if (x + y) % 2 == 0:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['grip_dark'])\n\n    # === FRAME (connecting grip to cylinder) - x: 9-12, y: 3-10 ===\n    for y in range(3, 11):\n        for x in range(9, 13):\n            if y == 3 or y == 10:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            else:\n                img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_medium'])\n\n    # === CYLINDER (large, bulging outward - key revolver feature) - x: 12-22, y: 1-12 ===\n    # The cylinder is wider than the frame, creating the distinctive revolver bulge\n    for y in range(1, 13):\n        for x in range(12, 23):\n            # Create elliptical cylinder shape\n            cy = 6.5  # center y\n            cx = 17   # center x\n            ry = 5.5  # radius y\n            rx = 5.5  # radius x\n\n            dx = (x - cx) / rx\n            dy = (y - cy) / ry\n            dist = dx * dx + dy * dy\n\n            if dist <= 1.0:\n                if dist > 0.75:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n                elif dist > 0.55:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n                elif y <= 4:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_light'])\n                elif y >= 9:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n                else:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_medium'])\n\n    # Cylinder chamber details (circles visible from top)\n    # Center chamber\n    img.putpixel((17, 6), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n    img.putpixel((17, 7), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n    # Surrounding chambers (visible from top as darker spots)\n    for cx, cy in [(15, 4), (19, 4), (15, 9), (19, 9)]:\n        img.putpixel((cx, cy), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n\n    # === BARREL (thick, short for 12.7mm) - x: 22-33, y: 4-9 ===\n    for y in range(4, 10):\n        for x in range(22, 33):\n            # Only draw if not already part of cylinder\n            px = img.getpixel((x, y))\n            if px == COLORS['transparent'] or x >= 23:\n                if y == 4 or y == 9:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n                elif y == 5:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_light'])\n                elif y == 8:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n                else:\n                    img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_medium'])\n\n    # Muzzle tip\n    img.putpixel((33, 5), COLORS['black'])\n    img.putpixel((33, 6), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n    img.putpixel((33, 7), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n    img.putpixel((33, 8), COLORS['black'])\n\n    # Front sight\n    img.putpixel((32, 5), COLORS['lighter_gray'])\n    img.putpixel((32, 8), COLORS['lighter_gray'])\n\n    # Rear sight (on frame, behind cylinder)\n    img.putpixel((10, 4), COLORS['lighter_gray'])\n    img.putpixel((10, 9), COLORS['lighter_gray'])\n\n    return img\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    # Create sprites\n    icon = create_revolver_icon()\n    topdown = create_revolver_topdown()\n\n    # Save to experiments folder first\n    icon.save('experiments/revolver_icon.png')\n    topdown.save('experiments/revolver_topdown.png')\n\n    print(f\"Created revolver_icon.png: {icon.size}\")\n    print(f\"Created revolver_topdown.png: {topdown.size}\")\n\n    # Also save to assets folder\n    icon.save('assets/sprites/weapons/revolver_icon.png')\n    topdown.save('assets/sprites/weapons/revolver_topdown.png')\n\n    print(\"\\nSprites saved to:\")\n    print(\"  -           "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nExtend the RSh-12 revolver barrel length by 2x.\nIssue #646: Make the revolver barrel 2 times longer.\n\nThis script modifies the existing revolver sprites to extend the barrel length.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom PIL import Image\n\n# Color palette from create_revolver_sprites.py\nCOLORS = {\n    'black': (30, 30, 30, 255),\n    'dark_gray': (45, 45, 45, 255),\n    'medium_gray': (60, 60, 60, 255),\n    'light_gray': (70, 70, 70, 255),\n    'lighter_gray': (90, 90, 90, 255),\n    'highlight': (100, 100, 100, 255),\n    'metal_dark': (35, 35, 40, 255),\n    'metal_medium': (50, 50, 55, 255),\n    'metal_light': (70, 70, 75, 255),\n    'grip_dark': (50, 40, 30, 255),\n    'grip_medium': (70, 55, 40, 255),\n    'grip_light': (85, 70, 50, 255),\n    'transparent': (0, 0, 0, 0),\n}\n\n\ndef extend_icon_barrel(original_img):\n    \"\"\"\n    Extend the icon barrel from ~25 pixels to ~50 pixels (2x).\n    Original barrel: x 50-75\n    New barrel: x 50-100\n\n    The image will grow from 80x24 to ~105x24\n    \"\"\"\n    orig_width, height = original_img.size\n    barrel_extension = 25  # Add 25 pixels to double the barrel length\n    new_width = orig_width + barrel_extension\n\n    # Create new image with extended width\n    new_img = Image.new('RGBA', (new_width, height), COLORS['transparent'])\n\n    # Copy all pixels from original, but shift the barrel part to the right\n    for y in range(height):\n        for x in range(orig_width):\n            pixel = original_img.getpixel((x, y))\n            if x < 50:\n                # Copy grip, frame, and cylinder as-is\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), pixel)\n            elif x >= 50:\n                # Shift barrel to the right by barrel_extension\n                new_img.putpixel((x + barrel_extension, y), pixel)\n\n    # Fill the gap with extended barrel (x: 50-75)\n    # This extends the barrel body\n    for x in range(50, 75):\n        for y in range(5, 12):\n            # Top edge\n            if y == 5:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            # Bottom edge\n            elif y == 11:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            # Barrel body shading\n            elif y == 6:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_light'])\n            elif y == 10:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n            elif y == 7:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['lighter_gray'])\n            else:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_medium'])\n\n    # Extend the under-barrel lug\n    for y in range(11, 14):\n        for x in range(50, 68):\n            if y == 13:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            elif x == 50:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            else:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n\n    # Add ventilated rib slots on the extended barrel\n    for x in range(54, 73, 4):\n        new_img.putpixel((x, 6), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n        new_img.putpixel((x + 1, 6), COLORS['dark_gray'])\n\n    return new_img\n\n\ndef extend_topdown_barrel(original_img):\n    \"\"\"\n    Extend the topdown barrel from ~11 pixels to ~22 pixels (2x).\n    Original barrel: x 22-33\n    New barrel: x 22-44\n\n    The image will grow from 34x14 to ~45x14\n    \"\"\"\n    orig_width, height = original_img.size\n    barrel_extension = 11  # Add 11 pixels to double the barrel length\n    new_width = orig_width + barrel_extension\n\n    # Create new image with extended width\n    new_img = Image.new('RGBA', (new_width, height), COLORS['transparent'])\n\n    # Copy all pixels from original, but shift the barrel part to the right\n    for y in range(height):\n        for x in range(orig_width):\n            pixel = original_img.getpixel((x, y))\n            if x < 22:\n                # Copy grip, frame, and cylinder as-is\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), pixel)\n            elif x >= 22:\n                # Shift barrel to the right by barrel_extension\n                new_img.putpixel((x + barrel_extension, y), pixel)\n\n    # Fill the gap with extended barrel (x: 22-33)\n    for x in range(22, 33):\n        for y in range(4, 10):\n            # Top edge\n            if y == 4:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            # Bottom edge\n            elif y == 9:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n            # Barrel body shading\n            elif y == 5:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_light'])\n            elif y == 8:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n            else:\n                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_medium'])\n\n    return new_img\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    # Load original sprites\n    icon_path = 'assets/sprites/weapons/revolver_icon.png'\n    topdown_path = 'assets/sprites/weapons/revolver_topdown.png'\n\n    print(\"Loading original sprites...\")\n    icon = Image.open(icon_path)\n    topdown = Image.open(topdown_path)\n\n    print(f\"Original icon size: {icon.size}\")\n    print(f\"Original topdown size: {topdown.size}\")\n\n    # Extend barrels\n    print(\"\\nExtending barrels by 2x...\")\n    new_icon = extend_icon_barrel(icon)\n    new_topdown = extend_topdown_barrel(topdown)\n\n    print(f\"New icon size: {new_icon.size}\")\n    print(f\"New topdown size: {new_topdown.size}\")\n\n    # Save to experiments folder for review\n    new_icon.save('experiments/revolver_icon_extended.png')\n    new_topdown.save('experiments/revolver_topdown_extended.png')\n\n    print(\"\\nExtended sprites saved to experiments folder:\")\n    print(\"  - experiments/revolver_icon_extended.png\")\n    print(\"  - experiments/revolver_topdown_extended.png\")\n\n    # Save to assets folder (replacing originals)\n    new_icon.save(icon_path)\n    new_topdown.save(topdown_path)\n\n    print(\"\\nOriginal sprites updated:\")\n    print(f\"  - {icon_path}\")\n    print(f\"  - {topdown_path}\")\n    print(\"\\nBarrel length extended by 2x successfully!\")\n"

original_img.size\n+    barrel_extension = 25  # Add 25 pixels to double the barrel length\n+    new_width = orig_width + barrel_extension\n+\n+    # Create new image with extended width\n+    new_img = Image.new('RGBA', (new_width, height), COLORS['transparent'])\n+\n+    # Copy all pixels from original, but shift the barrel part to the right\n+    for y in range(height):\n+        for x in range(orig_width):\n+            pixel = original_img.getpixel((x, y))\n+            if x < 50:\n+                # Copy grip, frame, and cylinder as-is\n+                new_img.putpixel((x, y), pixel)\n+            elif x >= 50:\n+                # Shift barrel to the right by barrel_extension\n+                new_img.putpixel((x + barrel_extension, y), pixel)\n+\n+    # Fill the gap with extended barrel (x: 50-75)\n+    # This extends the barrel body\n+    for x in range(50, 75):\n+        for y in range(5, 12):\n+            # Top edge\n+            if y == 5:\n+    - When you finalize the pull request:

      make sure no uncommitted changes corresponding to the original requirements are left behind,

GitHub CLI command patterns.
   - IMPORTANT: Always use --paginate flag when fetching lists from GitHub API to ensure all results are returned (GitHub returns max 30 per page by default).
   - When listing PR review comments (inline code comments), use gh api repos/OWNER/REPO/pulls/NUMBER/comments --paginate.
   - When listing PR conversation comments, use gh api repos/OWNER/REPO/issues/NUMBER/comments --paginate.
   - When listing PR reviews, use gh api repos/OWNER/REPO/pulls/NUMBER/reviews --paginate.
   - When listing issue comments, use gh api repos/OWNER/REPO/issues/NUMBER/comments --paginate.
   - When adding PR comment, use gh pr comment NUMBER --body "text" --repo OWNER/REPO.
   - When adding issue comment, use gh issue comment NUMBER --body "text" --repo OWNER/REPO.
   - When viewing PR details, use gh pr view NUMBER --repo OWNER/REPO.
   - When filtering with jq, use gh api repos/${owner}/${repo}/pulls/${prNumber}/comments --paginate --jq 'reverse | .[0:5]'.

Playwright MCP usage (browser automation via mcp__playwright__* tools).
   - When you develop frontend web applications (HTML, CSS, JavaScript, React, Vue, Angular, etc.), use Playwright MCP tools to test the UI in a real browser.
   - When WebFetch tool fails to retrieve expected content (e.g., returns empty content, JavaScript-rendered pages, or login-protected pages), use Playwright MCP tools (browser_navigate, browser_snapshot) as a fallback for web browsing.
   - When you need to interact with dynamic web pages that require JavaScript execution, use Playwright MCP tools.
   - When you need to visually verify how a web page looks or take screenshots, use browser_take_screenshot from Playwright MCP.
   - When you need to fill forms, click buttons, or perform user interactions on web pages, use Playwright MCP tools (browser_click, browser_type, browser_fill_form).
   - When you need to test responsive design or different viewport sizes, use browser_resize from Playwright MCP.
   - When you finish using the browser, always close it with browser_close to free resources.

Visual UI work and screenshots.
   - When you work on visual UI changes (frontend, CSS, HTML, design), include a render or screenshot of the final result in the pull request description.
   - When you need to show visual results, take a screenshot and save it to the repository (e.g., in a docs/screenshots/ or assets/ folder).
   - When you save screenshots to the repository, use permanent raw file links in the pull request description markdown (e.g., https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Jhon-Crow/godot-topdown-MVP/issue-646-7ea9af97780e/docs/screenshots/result.png).
   - When uploading images, commit them to the branch first, then reference them using the raw GitHub URL format.
   - When the visual result is important for review, mention it explicitly in the pull request description with the embedded image.

  "type": "user",
  "message": {
    "role": "user",
    "content": [
      {
        "tool_use_id": "toolu_01JsEEgjTioZXA9Sh7SD6NNM",
        "type": "tool_result",
        "content": "diff --git a/assets/sprites/weapons/revolver_icon.png b/assets/sprites/weapons/revolver_icon.png\nindex 060ea8a4..f4ce871a 100644\nBinary files a/assets/sprites/weapons/revolver_icon.png and b/assets/sprites/weapons/revolver_icon.png differ\ndiff --git a/assets/sprites/weapons/revolver_topdown.png b/assets/sprites/weapons/revolver_topdown.png\nindex e6c703e1..a0ba087f 100644\nBinary files a/assets/sprites/weapons/revolver_topdown.png and b/assets/sprites/weapons/revolver_topdown.png differ\ndiff --git a/experiments/extend_revolver_barrel.py b/experiments/extend_revolver_barrel.py\nnew file mode 100644\nindex 00000000..2be0fa1f\n--- /dev/null\n+++ b/experiments/extend_revolver_barrel.py\n@@ -0,0 +1,174 @@\n+#!/usr/bin/env python3\n+\"\"\"\n+Extend the RSh-12 revolver barrel length by 2x.\n+Issue #646: Make the revolver barrel 2 times longer.\n+\n+This script modifies the existing revolver sprites to extend the barrel length.\n+\"\"\"\n+\n+from PIL import Image\n+\n+# Color palette from create_revolver_sprites.py\n+COLORS = {\n+    'black': (30, 30, 30, 255),\n+    'dark_gray': (45, 45, 45, 255),\n+    'medium_gray': (60, 60, 60, 255),\n+    'light_gray': (70, 70, 70, 255),\n+    'lighter_gray': (90, 90, 90, 255),\n+    'highlight': (100, 100, 100, 255),\n+    'metal_dark': (35, 35, 40, 255),\n+    'metal_medium': (50, 50, 55, 255),\n+    'metal_light': (70, 70, 75, 255),\n+    'grip_dark': (50, 40, 30, 255),\n+    'grip_medium': (70, 55, 40, 255),\n+    'grip_light': (85, 70, 50, 255),\n+    'transparent': (0, 0, 0, 0),\n+}\n+\n+\n+def extend_icon_barrel(original_img):\n+    \"\"\"\n+    Extend the icon barrel from ~25 pixels to ~50 pixels (2x).\n+    Original barrel: x 50-75\n+    New barrel: x 50-100\n+\n+    The image will grow from 80x24 to ~105x24\n+    \"\"\"\n+    orig_width, height = original_img.size\n+    barrel_extension = 25  # Add 25 pixels to double the barrel length\n+    new_width = orig_width + barrel_extension\n+\n+    # Create new image with extended width\n+    new_img = Image.new('RGBA', (new_width, height), COLORS['transparent'])\n+\n+    # Copy all pixels from original, but shift the barrel part to the right\n+    for y in range(height):\n+        for x in range(orig_width):\n+            pixel = original_img.getpixel((x, y))\n+            if x < 50:\n+                # Copy grip, frame, and cylinder as-is\n+                new_img.putpixel((x, y), pixel)\n+            elif x >= 50:\n+                # Shift barrel to the right by barrel_extension\n+                new_img.putpixel((x + barrel_extension, y), pixel)\n+\n+    # Fill the gap with extended barrel (x: 50-75)\n+    # This extends the barrel body\n+    for x in range(50, 75):\n+        for y in range(5, 12):\n+            # Top edge\n+            if y == 5:\n+                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n+            # Bottom edge\n+            elif y == 11:\n+                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n+            # Barrel body shading\n+            elif y == 6:\n+                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_light'])\n+            elif y == 10:\n+                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n+            elif y == 7:\n+                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['lighter_gray'])\n+            else:\n+                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_medium'])\n+\n+    # Extend the under-barrel lug\n+    for y in range(11, 14):\n+        for x in range(50, 68):\n+            if y == 13:\n+                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n+            elif x == 50:\n+                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['black'])\n+            else:\n+                new_img.putpixel((x, y), COLORS['metal_dark'])\n+\n+    #
